(******************************************************************************************

 The collage of an enriched profunctor

 A fundamental construction on enriched profunctors is given by the collage (also known as
 the cograph). The collage of an enriched profunctor `E₁ ↛e E₂` is given by the enriched
 category defined as follows:
 - objects: `E₁ ⨿ E₂`
 - morphisms from `x₁ : E₁` to `x₂ : E₁`: morphisms in `E₁`
 - morphisms from `y₁ : E₂` to `x₂ : E₁`: morphisms from `I_{V}` to the initial object
 - morphisms from `x₁ : E₁` to `y₂ : E₂`: `I_{V} --> P y₁ x₁`
 - morphisms from `y₁ : E₂` to `y₂ : E₂`: morphisms in `E₂`
 Essentially, the morphisms between objects from `E₁` are given by morphisms in `E₂`, and
 similarly for `E₂`. Morphisms from an object in `E₁` to an object `E₂` are determined by
 the profunctor `P`, whereas morphisms from an object in `E₂` to an object in `E₁` are given
 by the initial object. If we were looking at set-enriched profunctors, then there would be
 no morphisms from something in `E₂` to something in `E₁`.

 In this file, we define the collage of an enriched profunctor, and we show that it gives
 rise to an opspan whose legs are fully faithful enriched functors. In addition, we show
 that under mild assumptions this gives rise to a univalent category (the assumption being
 that there is no morphism from the unit of the monoidal category to the initial object).
 Note that the collage of a profunctor is an instance of a colimit. As such, if the
 aforementioned condition is not satisfied, then we could take its Rezk completion to
 acquire the desired univalent category (where, if necessary, we need to mind a potential
 increase in the universe level).

 References
 - "Fibrations in bicategories" by Street
 - "Categorical notions of fibration" by Loregian and Riehl

 Content
 1. The underlying category
 2. The enrichment
 3. The underlying category
 4. The underlying category is univalent
 5. The left inclusion
 6. The right inclusion
 7. The square of the collage

 ******************************************************************************************)

enriched_comp
  enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment_data x₂ x₃ x₄
#⊗ identity
     (enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment_data
      ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
· enriched_comp
    enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment_data x₁ x₂
    x₄ =

  (enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment_data ⦃ x₃,
   x₄ ⦄)
  (enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment_data ⦃ x₂,
   x₃ ⦄)
  (enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment_data ⦃ x₁,
   x₂ ⦄)
· identity
    (enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment_data ⦃ x₃,
     x₄ ⦄)
  #⊗ enriched_comp
       enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment_data x₁
       x₂ x₃
· enriched_comp
    enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment_data x₁ x₃
    x₄

enriched_comp E₁ x₂ x₃ x₄ #⊗ identity (P y₁ x₂)
· rmap_e P y₁ x₂ x₄ =
mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₄ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄)
  (P y₁ x₂)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₄ ⦄) #⊗ rmap_e P y₁ x₂ x₃
· rmap_e P y₁ x₃ x₄
 apply rmap_e_comp.
      
V: benabou_cosmos
C₁, C₂: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
P: enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
IV:= benabou_cosmos_initial V: Initial V
y₁: C₂
x₂, x₃: C₁
y₄: C₂
arrow_from_tensor_initial_r_benabou_cosmos
  (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄) IV #⊗ identity (P y₁ x₂)
· arrow_from_tensor_initial_r_benabou_cosmos (P y₁ x₂)
    (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₄ ⦄) =
mon_lassociator IV (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄) (P y₁ x₂)
· identity IV #⊗ rmap_e P y₁ x₂ x₃
· arrow_from_tensor_initial_r_benabou_cosmos (P y₁ x₃)
    (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₄ ⦄)
 use arrow_from_tensor_initial_1_benabou_cosmos_eq.

· (mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₄ ⦄)
     (P y₂ x₃)
   · (mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₄ ⦄)
        (P y₂ x₃)
      · (sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
           ((E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₄ ⦄) ⊗ P y₂ x₃)
         · (mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₄ ⦄) (P y₂ x₃)
              (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
            · (identity (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₄ ⦄)
               #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (P y₂ x₃)
                    (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
               · (mon_rassociator (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₄ ⦄)
                    (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (P y₂ x₃)
                  · mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₄ ⦄)
                      (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (P y₂ x₃))))))) =
?b

          
V: benabou_cosmos
C₁, C₂: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
P: enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
IV:= benabou_cosmos_initial V: Initial V
y₁, y₂: C₂
x₃, x₄: C₁
sym_mon_braiding V ((E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₄ ⦄) ⊗ P y₂ x₃)
  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₄ ⦄)
     (P y₂ x₃)
   · (mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₄ ⦄)
        (P y₂ x₃)
      · (sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
           ((E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₄ ⦄) ⊗ P y₂ x₃)
         · (mon_lassociator (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₄ ⦄) (P y₂ x₃)
              (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
            · (identity (E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₄ ⦄)
               #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (P y₂ x₃)
                    (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
               · identity
                   ((E₁ ⦃ x₃, x₄ ⦄)
                    ⊗ ((E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ P y₂ x₃))))))) =
?b

arrow_from_tensor_initial_r_benabou_cosmos (P y₂ x₃)
  (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₄ ⦄) #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₄ =
mon_lassociator IV (P y₂ x₃) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· identity IV
  #⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V (P y₂ x₃) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
      · lmap_e P y₂ y₁ x₃)
· arrow_from_tensor_initial_r_benabou_cosmos (P y₁ x₃)
    (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₄ ⦄)
 use arrow_from_tensor_initial_1_benabou_cosmos_eq.

x₄: C₁
(sym_mon_braiding V (P y₃ x₄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
 · lmap_e P y₃ y₂ x₄) #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V (P y₂ x₄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
   · lmap_e P y₂ y₁ x₄) =

  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· identity (P y₃ x₄) #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₃
· (sym_mon_braiding V (P y₃ x₄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₃ ⦄)
   · lmap_e P y₃ y₁ x₄)

V: benabou_cosmos
C₁, C₂: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
P: enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
IV:= benabou_cosmos_initial V: Initial V
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
x₄: C₁
mon_lassociator (P y₃ x₄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V (P y₃ x₄)
     ((E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
   · (sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
        (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) #⊗ identity (P y₃ x₄)
      · mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
          (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (P y₃ x₄)
      · identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) #⊗ lmap_e P y₃ y₂ x₄
      · lmap_e P y₂ y₁ x₄)) =
(sym_mon_braiding V (P y₃ x₄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
 · lmap_e P y₃ y₂ x₄) #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V (P y₂ x₄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
   · lmap_e P y₂ y₁ x₄)

        
V: benabou_cosmos
C₁, C₂: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
P: enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
IV:= benabou_cosmos_initial V: Initial V
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
x₄: C₁
mon_lassociator (P y₃ x₄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (P y₃ x₄)
    ((E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ identity (P y₃ x₄)
· mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
    (P y₃ x₄)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) #⊗ lmap_e P y₃ y₂ x₄
· lmap_e P y₂ y₁ x₄ =
(sym_mon_braiding V (P y₃ x₄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
 · lmap_e P y₃ y₂ x₄) #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (P y₂ x₄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· lmap_e P y₂ y₁ x₄


        
V: benabou_cosmos
C₁, C₂: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
P: enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
IV:= benabou_cosmos_initial V: Initial V
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
x₄: C₁
mon_lassociator (P y₃ x₄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (P y₃ x₄)
    ((E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ identity (P y₃ x₄)
· mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
    (P y₃ x₄)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) #⊗ lmap_e P y₃ y₂ x₄ =
(sym_mon_braiding V (P y₃ x₄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
 · lmap_e P y₃ y₂ x₄) #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (P y₂ x₄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)

  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V (P y₃ x₄)
     ((E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
   · (sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
        (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) #⊗ identity (P y₃ x₄)
      · (mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
           (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (P y₃ x₄)
         · identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
           #⊗ lmap_e P y₃ y₂ x₄))) =

#⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (lmap_e P y₃ y₂ x₄ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
   · sym_mon_braiding V (P y₂ x₄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))

C₁, C₂: category

IV:= benabou_cosmos_initial V: Initial V
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
x₄: C₁
mon_lassociator (P y₃ x₄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (P y₃ x₄)
    ((E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
· mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
    (P y₃ x₄)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (P y₃ x₄)
· mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (P y₃ x₄)
    (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V ((E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) ⊗ P y₃ x₄)
    (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) =
mon_lassociator (P y₃ x₄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (P y₃ x₄)
    ((E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ identity (P y₃ x₄)
· mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
    (P y₃ x₄)

  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V (P y₃ x₄)
     ((E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
   · (mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
        (P y₃ x₄)

         #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
              (P y₃ x₄)
         · (mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (P y₃ x₄)
              (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
            · sym_mon_braiding V
                ((E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) ⊗ P y₃ x₄)
                (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))))) =

           #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (P y₃ x₄)
                (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
         · mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
             (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (P y₃ x₄)
         · sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
             (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) #⊗ identity (P y₃ x₄)
         · mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
             (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (P y₃ x₄)))) = ?b

          
V: benabou_cosmos
C₁, C₂: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
P: enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
IV:= benabou_cosmos_initial V: Initial V
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
x₄: C₁
mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (P y₃ x₄)
  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (P y₃ x₄)
     (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
   · identity (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
     #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V (P y₃ x₄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
   · mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
       (P y₃ x₄)
   · sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
       (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) #⊗ identity (P y₃ x₄)
   · mon_lassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
       (P y₃ x₄)) = ?t2

enriched_comp E₂ y₂ y₃ y₄ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₄ =

  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· identity (E₂ ⦃ y₃, y₄ ⦄)
  #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₃
· enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₃ y₄
 apply enrichment_assoc.

  (enriched_from_arr
     enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment_data f) =
f

∏
(x y z : enriched_profunctor_collage_precategory_data)
(f : enriched_profunctor_collage_precategory_data ⟦ x,
     y ⟧)
(g : enriched_profunctor_collage_precategory_data ⟦ y,
     z ⟧),
f · g =
enriched_to_arr
  enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment_data
  (mon_linvunitor I_{ V}
   · enriched_from_arr
       enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment_data g
     #⊗ enriched_from_arr
          enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment_data
          f
   · enriched_comp
       enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment_data x y
       z)

g: V ⟦ I_{ V}, P y₂ x₃ ⟧
f · InitialArrow IV (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₃ ⦄) =
mon_linvunitor I_{ V}
· (identity I_{ V} #⊗ f · g #⊗ identity IV)
· arrow_from_tensor_initial_l_benabou_cosmos (P y₂ x₃)
    (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₃ ⦄)

g: V ⟦ I_{ V}, P y₂ x₃ ⟧
g · lmap_e_arr P x₃ f =
g
· (mon_rinvunitor (P y₂ x₃)
   · (identity (P y₂ x₃) #⊗ enriched_from_arr E₂ f
      · (sym_mon_braiding V (P y₂ x₃) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
         · lmap_e P y₂ y₁ x₃)))

        
V: benabou_cosmos
C₁, C₂: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
P: enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
IV:= benabou_cosmos_initial V: Initial V
y₁, y₂: C₂
x₃: C₁
f: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
g: V ⟦ I_{ V}, P y₂ x₃ ⟧
lmap_e_arr P x₃ f =
mon_rinvunitor (P y₂ x₃)
· (identity (P y₂ x₃) #⊗ enriched_from_arr E₂ f
   · (sym_mon_braiding V (P y₂ x₃) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
      · lmap_e P y₂ y₁ x₃))

V: benabou_cosmos
C₁, C₂: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
P: enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
IV:= benabou_cosmos_initial V: Initial V
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
f: C₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
f · g =
enriched_to_arr E₂
  (mon_linvunitor I_{ V}
   · enriched_from_arr E₂ g #⊗ enriched_from_arr E₂ f
   · enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₃)
 exact (enriched_to_arr_comp E₂ f g).
  Qed.

P: enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
IV:= benabou_cosmos_initial V: Initial V
H₁: is_univalent C₁
H₂: is_univalent C₂
HV: V ⟦ I_{ V}, IV ⟧ → ∅
x₁, x₂: C₁
p: inl x₁ = inl x₂
maponpaths inl (paths_inl_inl_equiv x₁ x₂ p) = p

        apply (homotinvweqweq (paths_inl_inl_equiv _ _)).

        apply (homotinvweqweq (paths_inr_inr_equiv _ _)).
  Qed.

  (** * 7. The square of the collage *)
  
V: benabou_cosmos

E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V

IV:= benabou_cosmos_initial V: Initial V
enriched_profunctor_square
  enriched_profunctor_collage_inl_enrichment
  enriched_profunctor_collage_inr_enrichment P
  (identity_enriched_profunctor
     enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment)

  
V: benabou_cosmos
C₁, C₂: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
P: enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
IV:= benabou_cosmos_initial V: Initial V
enriched_profunctor_square
  enriched_profunctor_collage_inl_enrichment
  enriched_profunctor_collage_inr_enrichment P
  (identity_enriched_profunctor
     enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment)

  (precomp_enriched_profunctor
     enriched_profunctor_collage_inl_enrichment
     enriched_profunctor_collage_inr_enrichment
     (identity_enriched_profunctor
        enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment))

  (λ (x : C₂) (y : C₁), identity (P x y))
 
V: benabou_cosmos
C₁, C₂: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
P: enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
IV:= benabou_cosmos_initial V: Initial V
∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₂) (y : C₁),
identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) #⊗ identity (P x₁ y)
· lmap_e
    (precomp_enriched_profunctor
       enriched_profunctor_collage_inl_enrichment
       enriched_profunctor_collage_inr_enrichment
       (identity_enriched_profunctor
          enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment)) x₁
    x₂ y = lmap_e P x₁ x₂ y · identity (P x₂ y)
V: benabou_cosmos
C₁, C₂: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
P: enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
IV:= benabou_cosmos_initial V: Initial V
∏ (x : C₂) (y₁ y₂ : C₁),
identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) #⊗ identity (P x y₁)
· rmap_e
    (precomp_enriched_profunctor
       enriched_profunctor_collage_inl_enrichment
       enriched_profunctor_collage_inr_enrichment
       (identity_enriched_profunctor
          enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment)) x
    y₁ y₂ = rmap_e P x y₁ y₂ · identity (P x y₂)

      
V: benabou_cosmos
C₁, C₂: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
P: enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
IV:= benabou_cosmos_initial V: Initial V
∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₂) (y : C₁),
identity (E₂ ⦃ x₂, x₁ ⦄) #⊗ identity (P x₁ y)
· lmap_e
    (precomp_enriched_profunctor
       enriched_profunctor_collage_inl_enrichment
       enriched_profunctor_collage_inr_enrichment
       (identity_enriched_profunctor
          enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment)) x₁
    x₂ y = lmap_e P x₁ x₂ y · identity (P x₂ y)
 abstract
          (intros ; cbn ;
           rewrite !tensor_id_id ;
           rewrite !id_left, id_right ;
           rewrite !assoc ;
           rewrite sym_mon_braiding_inv ;
           apply id_left).
      
V: benabou_cosmos
C₁, C₂: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
P: enriched_profunctor E₁ E₂
IV:= benabou_cosmos_initial V: Initial V
∏ (x : C₂) (y₁ y₂ : C₁),
identity (E₁ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) #⊗ identity (P x y₁)
· rmap_e
    (precomp_enriched_profunctor
       enriched_profunctor_collage_inl_enrichment
       enriched_profunctor_collage_inr_enrichment
       (identity_enriched_profunctor
          enriched_profunctor_collage_enrichment)) x
    y₁ y₂ = rmap_e P x y₁ y₂ · identity (P x y₂)
 abstract
          (intros ; cbn ;
           rewrite !tensor_id_id ;
           rewrite !id_left, id_right ;
           apply idpath).
  Defined.
